班	team; class; grade; (military) squad; work shift; CL:個|个[ge4]; classifier for groups of people and scheduled transport vehicles	魏无羡和蓝忘机是一班的同学，关系非常好。	Wei Wuxian and Lan Wangji are classmates in the same grade, and they have a very good relationship.	蓝曦臣负责领导这个救援班，组织大家进行救援工作。	Lan Xichen is responsible for leading this rescue team and organizing everyone for the rescue work.	温宁是这个班里最勤奋的人，大家都很佩服他。	Wen Ning is the most hardworking person in this group, and everyone admires him.
吃土	(neologism c. 2015) (slang) (used jokingly) to live on dirt (typically because one has spent all one's money on consumer items)	魏无羡又买了一堆酒，现在又得吃土了。	Wei Wuxian bought a bunch of alcohol again, now he's going to be broke.	蓝忘机劝告魏无羡不要再买奢侈品，免得吃土。	Lan Wangji advised Wei Wuxian not to buy luxury goods anymore, so he wouldn't end up broke.	温宁每次都帮助别人，结果自己总是吃土。	Wen Ning always helps others, but ends up broke himself.
烟	cigarette or pipe tobacco; CL:根[gen1]; smoke; mist; vapour; CL:縷|缕[lu:3]; tobacco plant; (of the eyes) to be irritated by smoke	魏无羡拿出一支烟，慢慢地点燃，吐出一口烟雾。	Wei Wuxian took out a cigarette, lit it slowly, and exhaled a puff of smoke.	蓝忘机不喜欢吸烟，因为烟会伤害身体。	Lan Wangji doesn't like smoking because it harms the body.	温青看到温宁在吸烟，忍不住责备他。	Wen Qing couldn't help but reprimand Wen Ning when she saw him smoking.
翼	wing; area surrounding the bullseye of a target; to assist; one of the 28 constellations of Chinese astronomy; old variant of 翌	蓝曦臣的剑法犹如翼般灵活，无往不利。	Lan Xichen's swordsmanship is as agile as a wing, invincible.	魏无羡的聪明才智是蓝忘机的翼，两人相辅相成。	Wei Wuxian's intelligence is Lan Wangji's wing, the two complement each other.	温青的医术就像温宁的翼，让他在江湖上立足。	Wen Qing's medical skills are like Wen Ning's wing, allowing him to establish himself in the martial world.
株	tree trunk; stump (tree root); a plant; classifier for trees or plants; strain (biology); to involve others (in shady business)	魏无羡和蓝忘机在树下坐着，树株旁边开满了鲜花。	Wei Wuxian and Lan Wangji sat under the tree, and flowers bloomed next to the tree trunk.	温青研究了这株草药很久，终于找到了解药。	Wen Qing studied this plant for a long time and finally found the antidote.	温宁在树株后面隐藏着，保护着他的家人。	Wen Ning hid behind the tree trunk, protecting his family.
白人饭	White People’s Food. hastily put together and pre-made meals commonly associated with white people, but also save time and money	魏无羡和江澄偷懒，只吃了一些白人饭。	Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng were lazy and only ate some pre-made meals.	金凌不喜欢吃白人饭，更喜欢自己动手做饭。	Jin Ling doesn't like eating pre-made meals and prefers to cook by himself.	蓝曦臣觉得白人饭虽然简单，但也很方便。	Lan Xichen thinks that pre-made meals, although simple, are also very convenient.

A person who is easily attracted to good-looking people or stars, sometimes to the extent of ignoring their weaknesses.	金凌被称为顏狗，因为他总是追星。	Jin Ling is called a "face dog" because he is always chasing after celebrities.	蓝忘机虽然英俊潇洒，但他不喜欢成为别人的顏狗。	Although Lan Wangji is handsome, he doesn't like to be someone's "face dog".	魏无羡不是顏狗，他更看重一个人的内在。	Wei Wuxian is not a "face dog"; he values a person's inner qualities more.

旁友	n. Beside+friend. Friend. This Internet slang term is a phonetic deviation of 朋友 [péng yǒu] “friend” and 胖友 [pàng yǒu] “fat friend.”	魏无羡和蓝忘机是很要好的旁友。	Wei Wuxian and Lan Wangji are very good friends.	金凌和蓝曦臣是两个旁友。	Jin Ling and Lan Xichen are two good friends.	魏无羡和江澄是多年的旁友。	Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng have been good friends for many years.
以上	that level or higher; that amount or more; the above-mentioned; (used to indicate that one has completed one's remarks) That is all.	以上就是我的意见。	That's all for my opinion.	以上是我的解释，希望你能理解。	That's my explanation above, I hope you can understand.	以上就是我的全部回答。	That's all my answer above.
松	loose; to loosen; to relax; floss (dry, fluffy food product made from shredded, seasoned meat or fish, used as a topping or filling)	蓝忘机的发髻松了下来。	Lan Wangji's bun loosened.	魏无羡喜欢在松软的草地上躺着。	Wei Wuxian likes to lie down on the soft grass.	江澄的腰带松了。	Jiang Cheng's belt loosened.
腦殘	adj. Brain+disabled. Literally “brain-damaged”, this slang term is often used to laugh at a person who is ludicrous, dumb, or weird.	他的行为真是脑残。	His behavior is really brain-damaged.	金光瑶的计划太脑残了。	Jin Guangyao's plan is too ludicrous.	魏无羡有时候也会做一些脑残的事情。	Sometimes Wei Wuxian also does some dumb things.
孝顺	filial; dutiful; devoted to one's parents (and grandparents etc); to show filial piety towards (an older family member); filial piety	蓝曦臣对哥哥蓝忘机很孝顺。	Lan Xichen is very filial to his brother, Lan Wangji.	温情对温宁很孝顺。	Wen Qing is very filial to Wen Ning.	金凌虽然脾气暴躁，但对舅舅很孝顺。	Although Jin Ling has a bad temper, he is very filial to his uncle.
起到	(in an expression of the form 起到…作用[qi3 dao4 xx5 zuo4 yong4]) to have (a (motivating etc) effect); to play (a (stabilizing etc) role)	蓝忘机的音乐起到了安抚魏无羡的作用。	Lan Wangji's music has a soothing effect on Wei Wuxian.	温情的话语起到了安抚温宁的作用。	Wen Qing's words played a role in comforting Wen Ning.	江澄的话起到了激励金凌的作用。	Jiang Cheng's words played a role in motivating Jin Ling.
小黃書	n. Little+yellow+book. The yellow little book is a nickname for books and magazines characterized by either pornography or eroticism.	金光瑶竟然在看小黄书！	Jin Guangyao is actually reading a little yellow book!	魏无羡偷偷藏了一本小黄书。	Wei Wuxian secretly hid a little yellow book.	蓝曦臣发现了蓝忘机的小黄书。	Lan Xichen found Lan Wangji's little yellow book.
通用	to use anywhere, anytime (card, ticket etc); to be used by everyone (language, textbook etc); (of two or more things) interchangeable	这种支付方式在全国范围内通用。	This payment method is universally accepted nationwide.	这本词典通用于初学者和高级学习者。	This dictionary is suitable for both beginners and advanced learners.	这个软件通用于各种操作系统。	This software is compatible with various operating systems.
軟妹	n. Soft+sister. Young women who are very feminine. Borrowed from the Japanese ACG culture, this Internet slang term is a little sexist	金凌喜欢软妹类型的女孩。	Jin Ling likes the soft sister type of girl.	魏无羡觉得软妹有点假。	Wei Wuxian thinks the soft sister type is a bit fake.	蓝忘机不太喜欢软妹。	Lan Wangji doesn't really like the soft sister type.
断	to break; to snap; to cut off; to give up or abstain from sth; to judge; (usu. used in the negative) absolutely; definitely; decidedly	蓝忘机断然拒绝了金光瑶的提议。	Lan Wangji decisively rejected Jin Guangyao's proposal.	魏无羡断了江澄的话。	Wei Wuxian cut off Jiang Cheng's words.	温情断定了这个药方的有效性。	Wen Qing judged the effectiveness of this prescription.

菇涼	n. Mushroom+cold. Girl. This Internet slang term is 姑娘 [gū niáng] “girl” in the Lanzhou dialect. It is often used for humorous effect.	蓝忘机对魏无羡说：“菇涼，你又调皮了。”	Lan Wangji said to Wei Wuxian, "Girl, you are mischievous again."	金凌调皮地对蓝曦臣喊：“菇涼，你快来看！”	Jin Ling mischievously called out to Lan Xichen, "Girl, come and see!"
跑	to run; to run away; to escape; to run around (on errands etc); (of a gas or liquid) to leak or evaporate; (verb complement) away; off	魏无羡看到蓝忘机，便跑了过去。	Wei Wuxian saw Lan Wangji and ran over.	江澄跑得很快，很快就追上了魏无羡。	Jiang Cheng ran very fast and quickly caught up with Wei Wuxian.	金凌跑到蓝曦臣身边，拉着他的袍子。	Jin Ling ran to Lan Xichen and tugged at his robe.
较	(bound form) to compare; (literary) to dispute; compared to; (before an adjective) relatively; comparatively; rather; also pr. [jiao3]	魏无羡较蓝忘机更擅长弹琴。	Wei Wuxian is more skilled at playing the qin compared to Lan Wangji.	蓝曦臣较江澄更善解人意。	Lan Xichen is more understanding compared to Jiang Cheng.	金凌较他的父亲更加倔强。	Jin Ling is more stubborn compared to his father.
化解	to dissolve; to resolve (contradictions); to dispel (doubts); to iron out (difficulties); to defuse (conflicts); to neutralize (fears)	蓝忘机总是能够化解魏无羡和江澄之间的矛盾。	Lan Wangji is always able to resolve the conflicts between Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng.	温情用智慧化解了蓝曦臣的疑虑。	Wen Qing used her wisdom to dispel Lan Xichen's doubts.	蓝忘机的出现化解了魏无羡心中的困惑。	Lan Wangji's appearance resolved the confusion in Wei Wuxian's heart.
送分題	n. Send+point+problem. Very easy question [on an exam]. This Internet slang term refers to question to which you must know the answer.	魏无羡对这个问题是送分题，轻而易举。	Wei Wuxian finds this question to be a giveaway, very easy.	蓝忘机觉得这道题是送分题，对他来说太简单了。	Lan Wangji thinks this question is a giveaway, too easy for him.	金凌觉得这是送分题，对他来说太简单了。	Jin Ling thinks this is a giveaway, too easy for him.
颠簸	to be jolted around (car on a bumpy road, boat on a rough sea, aircraft experiencing turbulence); (fig.) to undergo a rough experience	魏无羡在马车上颠簸了一整天，很是疲惫。	Wei Wuxian was jolted around in the carriage all day and felt very tired.	温宁在江湖上颠簸了一生，却从未放弃过。	Wen Ning underwent a rough experience in the jianghu all his life, but never gave up.	蓝曦臣的心情像船在海上颠簸一样，起起伏伏。	Lan Xichen's mood was like a boat jolting on the sea, fluctuating.
开花	to bloom; to blossom; to flower; (fig.) to burst; to split open; (fig.) to burst with joy; (fig.) to spring up everywhere; to flourish	蓝忘机的笑容就像春天的花朵一样开花。	Lan Wangji's smile is like a blooming flower in spring.	魏无羡的音乐让人心情愉悦，就像一朵花开花一样。	Wei Wuxian's music brings joy to people's hearts, just like a flower blooming.	温情的医术在古代医学界开花结果。	Wen Qing's medical skills flourished in the ancient medical community.
期	a period of time; phase; stage; classifier for issues of a periodical, courses of study; time; term; period; to hope; Taiwan pr. [qi2]	魏无羡在云深不知处度过了一段美好的期。	Wei Wuxian spent a wonderful period of time in the Burial Mounds.	蓝忘机的琴音让人仿佛穿越到了古代的期。	Lan Wangji's qin music makes people feel as if they have traveled back to ancient times.	温情在医学研究的期中取得了巨大的成就。	Wen Qing achieved great success in the middle of her medical research.
偏	to lean; to slant; oblique; prejudiced; to deviate from average; to stray from the intended line; stubbornly; contrary to expectations	魏无羡的性格有些偏激，但却很有个性。	Wei Wuxian's personality is somewhat extreme, but very distinctive.	蓝忘机的眼神有些偏冷，却隐藏着深情。	Lan Wangji's gaze is somewhat cold, but it hides deep affection.	温情的性格有些偏执，但对医学的执着却是无可挑剔的。	Wen Qing's personality is somewhat stubborn, but her dedication to medicine is impeccable.
粉丝	bean vermicelli; mung bean starch noodles; Chinese vermicelli; cellophane noodles; CL:把[ba3]; fan (loanword); enthusiast for sb or sth	魏无羡最喜欢吃的面条是粉丝。	Wei Wuxian's favorite noodles to eat are bean vermicelli.	蓝忘机不太喜欢吃粉丝，更喜欢面条。	Lan Wangji doesn't like to eat bean vermicelli very much, he prefers noodles.	温情做的粉丝汤是江湖上最好吃的。	Wen Qing's bean vermicelli soup is the most delicious in the jianghu.

(one's) type	魏无羡做的菜清淡可口，大家都很喜欢。	Wei Wuxian's dishes are light and delicious, and everyone likes them.	蓝忘机不擅长做菜，但他的烧饼却是一绝。	Lan Wangji is not good at cooking, but his pancakes are exceptional.	温情的菜色虽然简单，却总是让人回味无穷。	Wen Qing's dishes, though simple, always leave a lasting impression.

药	medicine; drug; substance used for a specific purpose (e.g. poisoning, explosion, fermenting); CL:種|种[zhong3],服[fu4],味[wei4]; to poison	魏无羡擅长炼制各种神奇的药物。	Wei Wuxian is skilled in refining various miraculous medicines.	温情的药引起了意想不到的副作用。	Wen Qing's medicine caused unexpected side effects.	蓝忘机的药对治疗鬼差有奇效。	Lan Wangji's medicine is remarkably effective in treating fierce corpses.
干	tree trunk; main part of sth; to manage; to work; to do; capable; cadre; to kill (slang); to fuck (vulgar); (coll.) pissed off; annoyed	魏无羡干了一番大事业，改变了整个江湖。	Wei Wuxian accomplished a great undertaking, changing the entire cultivation world.	蓝忘机干得漂亮，解决了这场危机。	Lan Wangji did a great job and resolved the crisis.	温情干得很出色，成为了医疗界的佼佼者。	Wen Qing did an excellent job and became an outstanding figure in the medical field.
急诊	to give or receive urgent medical treatment; emergency treatment (at a hospital emergency department, or from a doctor on a house call)	魏无羡受伤后被送往急诊室。	Wei Wuxian was taken to the emergency room after being injured.	温情是急诊室的主治医生，经常忙得不可开交。	Wen Qing is the attending physician in the emergency room and is often extremely busy.	蓝忘机在急诊室里接受了紧急手术。	Lan Wangji underwent emergency surgery in the emergency room.

打臉	v. To slap one’s own face. To behave in ways that contradict one’s previous statements; to have one’s claims contradicted by the truth.	魏无羡总是喜欢打臉，说话从来不负责任。	Wei Wuxian always likes to contradict himself, never taking responsibility for what he says.	蓝忘机的行为总是不会打臉他的承诺。	Lan Wangji's actions never contradict his promises.	温情不会打臉自己的原则，一贯坚持自己的立场。	Wen Qing never contradicts her own principles and always sticks to her position.
甜寵	“sweet and pampering” idol dramas which are replete with sweet romantic scenes where the male lead would do anything for the female lead	金凌喜欢看甜宠剧，总是为男女主角的爱情故事感动。	Jin Ling likes to watch sweet and pampering idol dramas and is always moved by the love stories of the male and female leads.	蓝曦臣不屑于看甜宠剧，觉得那是浪费时间。	Lan Xichen disdains watching sweet and pampering idol dramas, considering it a waste of time.	魏无羡偶尔也会看甜宠剧，但从不愿承认。	Wei Wuxian occasionally watches sweet and pampering idol dramas, but never admits it.

抖森	n. Tremble+forest. This Internet slang term is a nickname for Tom Hiddleston because it sounds a little like his last name “Hiddleston.”	抖森在演技方面有着出色的表现。	Tom Hiddleston has excellent performance in acting.	抖森的粉丝们对他的新电影充满期待。	Tom Hiddleston's fans are looking forward to his new movie.	抖森因出色的表演而备受赞誉。	Tom Hiddleston is highly praised for his excellent performance.

与其	rather than... (used in expressions of the form 與其|与其[yu3qi2] + {verb1} + 不如[bu4ru2] + {verb2} "rather than {verb1}, better to {verb2}")	与其等待，不如自己动手。	Rather than waiting, it's better to take action.	与其抱怨，不如努力改变。	Rather than complaining, it's better to work hard to change.	与其后悔，不如从错误中学习。	Rather than regretting, it's better to learn from mistakes.

鬥圖	v. Compete+pictures. To bicker or joke using pictures. This Internet slang term refers to having a playful pictorial conversation online.	魏无羡和江澄經常在群裡鬥圖。	Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng often bicker using pictures in the group chat.	蓝忘机和蓝曦臣鬥圖，逗得全群人哈哈大笑。	Lan Wangji and Lan Xichen joke using pictures, making everyone in the group laugh.	金凌和泥萌互相鬥圖，把朋友逗得前仰后合。	Jin Ling and the others compete using pictures, making their friends laugh heartily.
吸霾	v. Sniff+smog. To have to sniff smog constantly because of air pollution. This Internet slang term mimics the word 吸煙 [xī yān] “smoking.”	魏无羡在那個城市吸霾，讓他很不舒服。	Wei Wuxian constantly sniffs smog in that city, which makes him very uncomfortable.	蓝忘机不喜歡吸霾，所以他很討厭這個城市。	Lan Wangji doesn't like sniffing smog, so he really dislikes this city.	泥萌每天都要吸霾，對身體很不好。	You guys have to sniff smog every day, which is very bad for your health.
泥萌	pron. Mud+cute. You guys. This Internet slang term is a phonetic deviation of 你們 [nǐ men] “you guys.” This term is often used humorously.	魏无羡對泥萌說：“你們這些小傢伙，又來搗亂了！”	Wei Wuxian said to you guys, "You little troublemakers are causing trouble again!"	蓝曦臣對泥萌們說：“你們這些小傢伙，別再亂跑了！”	Lan Xichen said to you guys, "You little troublemakers, stop running around!"	金凌對泥萌們說：“你們這些小傢伙，別再鬧了！”	Jin Ling said to you guys, "You little troublemakers, stop making a fuss!"
無感	adj. No feeling. Show no interest. To be not affected. This Internet slang term is used to show your disinterest in someone or something.	魏无羡對江澄的挑釁無感，繼續自顧自地玩著。	Wei Wuxian showed no interest in Jiang Cheng's provocation and continued to play by himself.	蓝忘机對蓝曦臣的玩笑無感，繼續專心工作。	Lan Wangji showed no interest in Lan Xichen's joke and continued to focus on his work.	金凌對泥萌的抱怨無感，繼續享受著美食。	Jin Ling showed no interest in your complaints and continued to enjoy the food.

This expression is often used to show one’s confidence about one’s ability or argument.	魏无羡對江澄說：“你不服憋著，我這招讓你見識見識！”	Wei Wuxian said to Jiang Cheng, "If you're not convinced, hold it in. Let me show you my move!"	蓝忘机對蓝曦臣說：“你不服憋著，我這一招讓你刮目相看！”	Lan Wangji said to Lan Xichen, "If you're not convinced, hold it in. Let me impress you with this move!"	金凌對泥萌說：“你們不服憋著，我這一招讓你們刮目相看！”	Jin Ling said to you guys, "If you're not convinced, hold it in. Let me impress you with this move!"

扶墻	v. To support myself by holding onto the wall. This Internet slang term describes one’s shock at something that rendered himself or herself unsteady.	魏无羡看到蓝忘机时，差点扶墙。	Wei Wuxian almost had to support himself by holding onto the wall when he saw Lan Wangji.	蓝曦臣扶墙而立，面色平静。	Lan Xichen stood by the wall, with a calm expression.	江澄扶墙而立，心中却是波涛汹涌。	Jiang Cheng stood by the wall, but his heart was in turmoil.
香	fragrant; sweet smelling; aromatic; savory or appetizing; (to eat) with relish; (of sleep) sound; perfume or spice; joss or incense stick; CL:根[gen1]	魏无羡闻到蓝忘机身上的香味，心中一暖。	Wei Wuxian smelled the fragrance on Lan Wangji's body, and felt warm in his heart.	蓝曦臣的茶香扑鼻，让人心旷神怡。	The aroma of Lan Xichen's tea is refreshing and delightful.	金凌偷偷闻了一下香，心中充满了幸福感。	Jin Ling secretly smelled the fragrance and felt a sense of happiness in his heart.
所	actually; place; classifier for houses, small buildings, institutions etc; that which; particle introducing a relative clause or passive; CL:個|个[ge4]	蓝忘机所到之处，无不留下深刻的印记。	Wherever Lan Wangji goes, he leaves a deep impression.	魏无羡所言不虚，他说的都是事实。	What Wei Wuxian says is not false; everything he says is the truth.	金凌所见所闻，让他对莫玄羽产生了好奇。	What Jin Ling saw and heard made him curious about Mo Xuanyu.
老濕	n. Always+wet. Teacher. This Internet slang term and 老師 [lǎo shī] “teacher” are homophones, but it is often used to refer to a lecherous male teacher.	蓝曦臣发现了学校里的老湿，立刻报告给了蓝忘机。	Lan Xichen discovered the lecherous male teacher in the school and immediately reported it to Lan Wangji.	魏无羡对老湿的行为感到愤怒，决定揭露他的真面目。	Wei Wuxian was angry about the lecherous teacher's behavior and decided to expose his true colors.	金凌不喜欢老湿，总是躲着他。	Jin Ling doesn't like the lecherous teacher and always avoids him.
大事	major event; major political event (war or change of regime); major social event (wedding or funeral); (do sth) in a big way; CL:件[jian4],樁|桩[zhuang1]	蓝忘机不喜欢参与大事，更喜欢安静的修炼。	Lan Wangji doesn't like to participate in major events; he prefers quiet cultivation.	魏无羡总是把大事看得很开，不喜欢被琐事困扰。	Wei Wuxian always takes major events lightly and doesn't like to be bothered by trivial matters.	蓝曦臣认为这是一件大事，必须要亲自出马。	Lan Xichen thinks this is a major event and must personally take action.
闹	noisy; cacophonous; to make noise; to disturb; to vent (feelings); to fall ill; to have an attack (of sickness); to go in (for some activity); to joke	魏无羡和江澄在莲花坞闹了一整天，玩得不亦乐乎。	Wei Wuxian and Jiang Cheng made a lot of noise in Lotus Pier all day, having a great time.	金凌不喜欢闹市区，更喜欢安静的地方。	Jin Ling doesn't like noisy urban areas; he prefers quiet places.	蓝曦臣不喜欢闹别扭，总是尽量维持和谐的氛围。	Lan Xichen doesn't like to make a fuss and always tries to maintain a harmonious atmosphere.
批	to ascertain; to act on; to criticize; to pass on; classifier for batches, lots, military flights; tier (for the ranking of universities and colleges)	蓝忘机对魏无羡的行为进行了批评，希望他能改正。	Lan Wangji criticized Wei Wuxian's behavior, hoping he would correct it.	蓝曦臣对弟弟的决定进行了批准，支持他的选择。	Lan Xichen approved his brother's decision and supported his choice.	金凌对自己的表现进行了批评，决定要更加努力。	Jin Ling criticized his own performance and decided to work even harder.

To hurt the feelings of single people [single dogs] knowingly or unknowingly through myriad forms of public display of affection.	魏无羡和蓝忘机的甜蜜互动，让金凌感到了花式虐狗。	The sweet interaction between Wei Wuxian and Lan Wangji made Jin Ling feel emotionally hurt as a single person.	蓝曦臣不喜欢花式虐狗，总是尽量避免在单身朋友面前过分秀恩爱。	Lan Xichen doesn't like to hurt the feelings of single people through excessive public display of affection and always tries to avoid it in front of his single friends.	魏无羡故意在江澄面前花式虐狗，逗得他哭笑不得。	Wei Wuxian deliberately hurt Jiang Cheng's feelings as a single person through excessive public display of affection, leaving him at a loss whether to laugh or cry.

大表哥	n. The eldest cousin brother. This Internet slang term is an affectionate nickname for British actor Dan Stevens, because of his role on Downton Abbey.	魏无羡是大表哥，他对江澄和金凌都很照顾。	Wei Wuxian is the eldest cousin brother, and he takes good care of Jiang Cheng and Jin Ling.	蓝曦臣在剑法上是大表哥，他的指导让许多人受益。	Lan Xichen is the eldest cousin brother in swordsmanship, his guidance has benefited many people.	金凌对大表哥魏无羡的敬仰溢于言表。	Jin Ling's admiration for his eldest cousin brother Wei Wuxian is beyond words.
先	beforehand; first; earlier; at first; originally; for the time being; for now; (prefix) my late (in referring to deceased relatives older than oneself)	咱们先去云深不知处，再商量对策。	Let's go to the Cloud Recesses first, and then discuss our countermeasures.	先不要生气，听我解释。	Don't be angry first, listen to my explanation.	先把这个问题搞清楚再说。	First, let's clarify this issue before we talk.
咱们	we or us (including both the speaker and the person(s) spoken to); (dialect) I or me; (dialect) (in a coaxing or familiar way) you; also pr. [za2 men5]	咱们一起去莲花坞吃饭吧。	Let's go to Lotus Pier to eat together.	咱们这就动身，不要耽搁时间。	Let's set off now, don't waste time.	咱们都是一家人，应该互相帮助。	We are all family, we should help each other.
照	according to; in accordance with; to shine; to illuminate; to reflect; to look at (one's reflection); to take (a photo); photo; as requested; as before	按照规定，大家都要遵守秩序。	According to the regulations, everyone must follow the order.	照镜子的时候，他突然笑了。	When he looked in the mirror, he suddenly smiled.	照这个方向走，就能找到蓝忘机了。	Follow this direction, and you will find Lan Wangji.
逗	to tease (playfully); to entice; (coll.) to joke; (coll.) funny; amusing; to stay; to sojourn; brief pause at the end of a phrase (variant of 讀|读[dou4])	魏无羡喜欢逗弄蓝忘机，让他不知所措。	Wei Wuxian likes to tease Lan Wangji, making him at a loss.	他的幽默感总能逗笑身边的人。	His sense of humor always amuses the people around him.	逗留在这里的时间不宜过长。	The time to stay here should not be too long.

尬舞	(slang) to battle each other in street dancing (derived from Taiwanese 較, which sounds similar to Mandarin 尬[ga4]); (slang) to perform weird dance moves	他们在舞台上尬舞，吸引了无数粉丝。	They battled each other in street dancing on stage, attracting countless fans.	尬舞的风格很独特，让人眼前一亮。	The style of weird dance moves is very unique, it's eye-catching.	他们尬舞的视频在网上走红了。	The video of their weird dance moves became popular online.
狼系男	n. Wolflike man. A wolflike man is calm, domineering, committed, and a bit hard to control. This slang term is often used to label a type of boyfriends.	她的男朋友是典型的狼系男，总是给她一种安全感。	Her boyfriend is a typical wolflike man, always giving her a sense of security.	他虽然是狼系男，但对朋友们总是很温柔。	Although he is a wolflike man, he is always very gentle with his friends.	狼系男的魅力在于他们的自信和果断。	The charm of wolflike men lies in their confidence and decisiveness.
雙標狗	n. Double standard+dog. A double-standard dog. This Internet slang term is a derogatory term for people who are considered practicing a double standard.	他总是对别人指手画脚，简直就是个雙標狗。	He always points fingers at others, he's simply a double-standard dog.	别听他的，他就是个雙標狗，自己却做得更过分。	Don't listen to him, he's just a double-standard dog, but he's even more excessive himself.	她讨厌那些雙標狗，总是说一套做一套。	She hates those double-standard dogs, always saying one thing and doing another.
不服來戰	<Expression> If you are not convinced, come and fight [come argue with me]. This expression is often used to show one’s confidence about one’s argument.	魏无羡对自己的观点很有信心，经常说不服来战。	Wei Wuxian is very confident in his views and often says "if you are not convinced, come and fight".	他的自信让他经常说出不服来战的话。	His confidence often leads him to say "if you are not convinced, come and fight".	不服来战，我一定能说服你。	If you are not convinced, come and fight, I will definitely persuade you.

開車	v. To drive a car. To talk dirty. The Internet slang term often describes harmless dirty jokes which probably would not be considered sexual harassment.	魏无羡开车的时候，总是放很劲的音乐。	Wei Wuxian always plays loud music when driving.	蓝忘机不擅长开车，但是他很喜欢收藏汽车模型。	Lan Wangji is not good at driving, but he loves collecting car models.	金凌学会了开车，但是他不喜欢在家人面前说脏话。	Jin Ling learned to drive, but he doesn't like to talk dirty in front of his family.
躁起來	<Expression> Get excited. Quoted from the song “Miss Dong” by Song Dongye, this expression is used to encourage people to become excited about something.	魏无羡一提起魏无羡，就躁起来，滔滔不绝。	When it comes to Wei Wuxian, he gets excited and talks non-stop.	蓝忘机听到音乐就躁起来，整个人都沉浸在音乐中。	Lan Wangji gets excited when he hears music, completely immersed in it.	金凌看到小狗就躁起来，忍不住想抱抱它。	Jin Ling gets excited when he sees a puppy and can't help but want to hug it.

污力滔滔	<Expression> Pouring out dirtiness in a steady flow. This expression is used to describe people who like talking about sex either directly or indirectly.	金光瑶污力滔滔地说着不堪入耳的话，让在场的人都感到尴尬。	Jin Guangyao kept pouring out dirty words that were unbearable to hear, making everyone present feel embarrassed.	魏无羡不喜欢和别人污力滔滔地聊天，他更喜欢开玩笑。	Wei Wuxian doesn't like chatting with others about sex; he prefers to make jokes.	蓝忘机不擅长应对别人污力滔滔的话题，他总是选择避而不谈。	Lan Wangji is not good at dealing with others pouring out dirty words; he always chooses to avoid the topic.
作为	one's conduct; deed; activity; accomplishment; achievement; to act as; as (in the capacity of); qua; to view as; to look upon (sth as); to take sth to be	蓝湛的作为总是让人感到惊讶，他总是能做到超乎寻常的事情。	Lan Zhan's deeds always surprise people; he can always do extraordinary things.	魏无羡的作为总是充满着正义感，他总是为了正义而努力。	Wei Wuxian's actions are always filled with a sense of justice; he always strives for justice.	金凌的作为总是让人感到骄傲，他总是能做出令人满意的成绩。

This Internet slang term is sometimes used humorously.	金凌有时候会装作生气，其实是个小戏精。	Sometimes Jin Ling pretends to be angry, but he's actually a little drama queen.	魏无羡有时候会故意逗蓝忘机生气，真是个大戏精。	Sometimes Wei Wuxian deliberately teases Lan Wangji to make him angry; he's really a big drama queen.	蓝曦臣虽然看起来沉稳，但有时也是个戏精。	Lan Xichen may look steady, but sometimes he's also a drama queen.
